< Text>
East Garden is a Chinese restaurant that offers Cantonese cuisine in the Guangzhou style. This four star rating is for their breakfast menu only, which is both fairly inexpensive and excellent: highly recommended are the beef rolls which consists of beef inside an almost crepe like wrapping of rice noodle. Another recommendation is their beef stew noodles soup, which has an excellent broth with chunks of beef, rice noodles and bok choy. They have a homemade spicy chili oil condiment which is great and works well with their soups.
As for the lunch and dinner menu, it is mostly forgettable.. honestly, I would give it two to three stars at best. Much of the dinner menu isn't great, some of it is less than fresh. BTW, vegetables are expensive here compared to their competition.
Service is fine. The owner is most often present.<//Text>

It‚Äôs a staple with my family and they suggested the shrimp rolls, which are essentially shrimp rolled ip in a pastry dough or maybe wonton wrapper, but let me say this, Delicious. Do not use this company, they are not ready to do what they are trying to do.</text>

< Text>
Very good management, keeps things clean and well run.  Prices seem competitive, but it is still expensive. However unlike some storage places, there is nobody on-site except during office hours. Some storage places alarm the individual units and key the alarm to the entry of the corresponding gate code. Not here.  So units are vulnerable to anyone with 60 seconds and a portable angle grinder, especially the outside units.  Another problem with the outside units: when they blow off the driveway a lot of dirt goes under the door into your unit.  I've had three separate units here and they all had that problem.  I still like this place, it's very convenient and the staff is excellent.  But I've seen better.</Text>
